As the highest Shangri-La hotel in the world, it is completely different from other traditional Shangri-La hotels. The lobby is on the 68th floor, the room is on the 78th floor, the gym is on the 71st floor, and the breakfast is on the 5th floor. Fortunately, I came from the Four Seasons Hotel in Guangzhou and I got used to it. The specially reserved 270-degree viewing room, to see the night view of Nanning at night, the sunrise in the morning, and the sunset in the evening, is indescribable.

The last one said that the shower room in the next room is in the center of the room, and it is transparent, which is really a bit embarrassing to use.
In short, the flaws are not concealed. As the latest and most upscale hotel in Nanning, it is strongly recommended.

Even if there is a charge, two bottles of mineral water are placed at the beginning, and they will be delivered after another. These attitudes are not in line with the high-end positioning of the hotel. It's rare in so many hotels. There was a small episode during my stay at the hotel. The design of the folding metal window next to the bathtub was very problematic. Because of the small space, it was easy to catch my hand. I was accidentally pinched, and my fingers were swollen immediately. I almost went to the hospital, and it's been four or five days and I'm still in pain. The hotel's attitude to solve this matter is to actively send medicine boxes and ice buckets, and then there is no more, which means that you deserve to clip it yourself anyway. As a traveler who has stayed in many, many top hotels, this solution can't be said to be irresponsible or anything wrong, I can only say that this is the most "standardized process" I have encountered, formulaic and indifferent.

Although Nanning Xiangji is a new hotel, the overall stay experience can be said to be full marks. Whether it is the front hall or guest room, or the Horizon Club and restaurant, the service staff I have encountered are generally very considerate and thoughtful, not too enthusiastic, but the details can reflect the well-trained. I ordered room delivery twice, one for fruit plate and cake, and one for Hainanese chicken rice. Although the two products are not amazing, they are within the standard. The variety of breakfast is not very rich, but it has everything that should be there. Except for the bad reviews of whole wheat toast, the other products are also above the standard. The happy hour of Horizon Club is from 5:30 to 7:30 in the evening. There are buffets and a la carte. There are a few types of pre-dinner snacks to choose from, but when the temperature suddenly drops, you can drink a bowl of Cordyceps flower stewed pork soup. It's so heartwarming and heartwarming.
The hotel's rooms are up to the 88th floor, but they are not yet open for use. This time I stayed in the Horizon Club Honor King Room on the 80th floor. I didn't take too many photos of the interior decoration of the room. You can go to a red book or other frequent guest apps to search. The hard fitting of the room is made of wood, which I personally like very much, it looks warm and warm. The view of the room and the landscape outside the window are comparable to that of the Dragon Light LC next door. The bathtub and sink in the room are from Villeroy & Boch, and the shower in the bathroom is from Hansgrohe. I need to complain that the design of the shower is a bit unreasonable. The toilet has TOTO's washlet, which is praised. The TV in the hotel is an 80-inch Huawei, which can project the screen and has a good definition. Of course, capsule coffee machines are also available. The only surprise is that there is no bluetooth speaker in the room, not even an alarm clock.
But in any case, this hotel should be the best hotel in Nanning so far in my opinion. The first time I wrote a review, it was a little messy. The rest of his good and bad, just wait for you to discover it yourself.
Nanning Fragrant Chicken, see you next time.
